<date>1620448450233<//date>< Rating>
5</Rating>
< text>
This is "food wise" an above-average Chinese Restaurant which I frequently visit. The folks here are charming and the portion size is, er, YUGE.

I highly recommend the Hot & Sour Soup (made by scratch on-site) as well as their Orange Chicken and the Wolf Fish (I've never heard of it but it's d-e-l-i-c-i-o-u-s!

Also, if you or your family walk in there with any kind of sweet tooth they have a wonderful bakery greeting you whence you first walk in the door.

The Proprietors are kindly and charming. This is a SUPERIOR DINING EXPERIENCE and I'm sure glad that they decided to do business here locally in Running Springs!

They have a patio dining area and live music on the weekends.

Go. You'll thank me.</text>

<userid>115614623232447959034</userid>< name>
Cao Thang</name>
< Time>
1606092923219< /Time>
<Rating>5< /Rating>< Review>
Can't find a better one... on the mountain. Or Even in the valley.

We got to sit in patios which they built very nicely and enjoyable.

The food entries are similar to Panda Express, except the taste is lighter which is suitable for people who's on diet or high blood pressure.

The soups were very good actually, we ordered chowder and egg drop soups, though all were good, the chowder has a richer taste and flavour which can be a good choice.

If you are a fan of beef, try smoked beef. It is very tender and high smoke flavor, it may look light and not so interested, but once you have the first peace, you will be amazed of how soft and rich it is, and unlike other place where smoked products usually tasty or salty, this is completely different.

I also love there taco tea and ginger tea. I'm an asian and have tried many places, taro milk tea is my favorite drink, and I felt in love with their milk tea. All tea are made with fresh and real ingredients, not from power like most of the tea shop out there. Tea were light and not too sweet, but the flavors is full and rich. Boba is very soft and tender too. Must try it.

Ah, plus: dont forget to try ginger tea, it's good and will keep you well in the cold weather of the mountain.

Enjoy your trip and meals.<//Review>

< text>
Can't find a better one... on the mountain. Or Even in the valley.

We got to sit in patios which they built very nicely and enjoyable.

The food entries are similar to Panda Express, except the taste is lighter which is suitable for people who's on diet or high blood pressure.

The soups were very good actually, we ordered chowder and egg drop soups, though all were good, the chowder has a richer taste and flavour which can be a good choice.

If you are a fan of beef, try smoked beef. It is very tender and high smoke flavor, it may look light and not so interested, but once you have the first peace, you will be amazed of how soft and rich it is, and unlike other place where smoked products usually tasty or salty, this is completely different.

I also love there taco tea and ginger tea. I'm an asian and have tried many places, taro milk tea is my favorite drink, and I felt in love with their milk tea. All tea are made with fresh and real ingredients, not from power like most of the tea shop out there. Tea were light and not too sweet, but the flavors is full and rich. Boba is very soft and tender too. Must try it.

Ah, plus: dont forget to try ginger tea, it's good and will keep you well in the cold weather of the mountain.

Enjoy your trip and meals.< /text>

<Text>Delicious food and great service make this restaurant an outstanding option for locals and folks traveling through Running Springs. Hilltop Chinese is great for kids and groups. 0x80c4abc1090cbeb9:0xc498ed77713b8202< /Gmap_id>
</record></dataset><record>
< Review>
I've been watching reviews and listening to feedback from other locals, and finally decided to try the food tonight. I'd add pictures, but devoured my meal without foresight.

As we walked in, a man working at a table welcomed us warmly, and was followed quickly by the counter staff. They are all very friendly, inviting and happy to answer any questions. We were offered samples and my otherwise simple decision became complicated. The pork was moist, tender and not overwhelmed by other flavors. I brought home orange chicken, honey walnut shrimp and broccoli beef, and was impressed by each.

As others have said, the honey walnut shrimp was delicious, and cooked to perfection. The Orange Chicken was a great choice - tender chicken with light breading and a perfect complement of orange sauce. The broccoli beef was cooked so well. The broccoli is very fresh, and only lightly steamed, so that the crisp stalk crunches as you bite through. I prefer this, and found it to be excellent. The beef melted in my mouth, and was almost in equal proportion to the amount of broccoli.

Running Springs has needed a variation on the restaurants we've had for years, and this perfectly answers the call. I can't wait to go back, and plan to bring all our friends and family!<//Review>

<review>Read other negative reviews, but decided to stop by anyway for our caffeine fix. We didn't encounter the surly barista; rather we were greeted by a nice young lady who was nothing but pleasant. I ordered green tea and JL ordered his standard chai latte. Both came out piping hot, which worked out well for our trek on the road. The walls were also loaded with lots of knick knacks and funny signs.

On the downside, there aren't any restrooms, no WiFi, and it's cash only. Boo! You still have the option of buying something at the market next door and getting cash back. Plus, you get to people watch folks coming in from the campsite next door. A feast for all of the senses.<//review>< Name>

< Review>
Unique and tasty concept of East-Indian style tandoori chicken and pizza. I had the lunch buffet which was less than $9 including tax, and included salad. I didn't get a drink, but it's just $1 extra if needed.

Overall, I give them a A- only because there wasn't any chai tea. If they had chai tea, I'd give this pizza place an A+ for sure!

There were 3 kinds of pizza out when I arrived, and they brought out more as people took the slices one by one. All together I had about 10 slices, and at least 5-6 different kinds of pizza in all. I remember 2 of the pizzas were vegetarian.

The lunch buffet is on weekdays only. The cashier told me it's from 11-2 Monday thru Friday. They're open 7 days a week, but I forgot to ask her the hours that their restaurant is open< /Review>

< Review>
This place was great. It is surprisingly spacious on the inside. The food comes out pretty fast and tastes amazing. Just a fair warning that their pizzas do have a bit of a kick so if you arent a fan of spicy of food this might not be the place for you. I really like how clean it is throughout the restaurant. I would highly recommend this place for friends and family.Seems like one of the best indian flavored pizzas. This place doesn't look like much from the outside or really the inside but let me tell you this was such an awesome treat for the three of us. We ordered 2 chicken korma, butter chicken, rice and bread and were so amazed at the flavors. And get this all that food and it was only $27 after tax. Would come here weekly if I lived here but we are from the Seattle area. Don't be fooled by the ordinary decor. The food in this place is so delicious that it has become our family's favorite take-out place in town. The service is excellent and the price quite fair for the quality and quality.< /Review>

Do yourself a favor, reserve a storage unit HERE!

Not only does it include amazing customer service by friendly, professional staff but it's also an affordable price for LA in a navigable location. Don't forget the convenience of managing your account online while having a flexible month to month contract :)

Obviously everyone knows that moving is stressful. My move was especially stressful, not because the fact I was moving from San Diego, but everything that you think could and couldn't go wrong...went wrong. From broken boxes from accident prone movers and sitting in traffic with empty gas tanks to wrong keys by missing landlords and ruined newly bought furniture and mishandled sentimental belongings- I begged the day to be over and naturally I dreaded my last stop:storage. Seriously I'm considering to believe in angels because when I went there, I easily spotted and found parking right away. I was greeted sincerely and helped right away! They worked with the movers and everything was stored and moved unbelievably smoothly! Words cannot express my gratitude and satisfaction. Thank you so much Stanley and Yesenia, I highly recommend you to go to this Public Storage unit!!<//Text>

Do yourself a favor, reserve a storage unit HERE!

Not only does it include amazing customer service by friendly, professional staff but it's also an affordable price for LA in a navigable location. Don't forget the convenience of managing your account online while having a flexible month to month contract :)

Obviously everyone knows that moving is stressful. My move was especially stressful, not because the fact I was moving from San Diego, but everything that you think could and couldn't go wrong...went wrong. From broken boxes from accident prone movers and sitting in traffic with empty gas tanks to wrong keys by missing landlords and ruined newly bought furniture and mishandled sentimental belongings- I begged the day to be over and naturally I dreaded my last stop:storage. It was heaven- the exact opposite of how my day was going.
Seriously I'm considering to believe in angels because when I went there, I easily spotted and found parking right away. I was greeted sincerely and helped right away! They worked with the movers and everything was stored and moved unbelievably smoothly! Words cannot express my gratitude and satisfaction. Thank you so much Stanley and Yesenia, I highly recommend you to go to this Public Storage unit!!< /Review>
